RÁPIDO:
🐧 comandos esenciales linux

referencia rápida pa los papus que usan linux

📁 navegación de archivos
# listar archivos
ls -la             # lista detallada con ocultos
ls -lh             # tamaños legibles (KB/MB)
ls -lt             # ordenado por fecha
ls -R              # recursivo (muestra subdirs)

# moverse
cd /ruta/absoluta   # ir a ruta absoluta
cd ../..           # subir 2 niveles
cd ~               # ir a home
cd -               # volver al directorio anterior
pwd                # mostrar directorio actual

# copiar/mover/borrar
cp archivo.txt dest/  # copiar archivo
cp -r carpeta/ dest/  # copiar carpeta recursivo
mv archivo.txt nuevo/  # mover/renombrar
rm archivo.txt       # borrar archivo
rm -rf carpeta/      # borrar carpeta (CUIDADO 💀)
mkdir -p a/b/c       # crear dirs anidados
touch archivo.txt    # crear archivo vacío
🔍 búsqueda
find / -name "archivo.txt"     # buscar por nombre
find . -name "*.iso"          # buscar ISOs en directorio actual
find / -size +1G              # archivos mayores a 1GB
find / -mtime -7              # modificados en últimos 7 días
grep -r "texto" /ruta/        # buscar texto en archivos
grep -n "texto" archivo       # mostrar número de línea
grep -i "TEXTO" archivo       # ignorar mayúsculas
locate archivo.txt            # búsqueda rápida (BD indexada)
which python3                 # ubicación de un comando
whereis nginx                 # binario + man + source
📦 gestores de paquetes
# ARCH/MANJARO/GARUDA (pacman)
sudo pacman -S paquete         # instalar
sudo pacman -Syu               # actualizar todo el sistema
sudo pacman -R paquete         # desinstalar
sudo pacman -Rs paquete        # desinstalar + dependencias
sudo pacman -Ss nombre         # buscar paquete
sudo pacman -Q                 # listar instalados
yay -S paquete-aur            # instalar desde AUR

# UBUNTU/DEBIAN/KALI (apt)
sudo apt update                # actualizar lista de paquetes
sudo apt upgrade               # actualizar paquetes instalados
sudo apt install paquete       # instalar
sudo apt remove paquete        # desinstalar
sudo apt autoremove            # limpiar huérfanos
apt search nombre              # buscar paquete
sudo dpkg -i archivo.deb       # instalar .deb manualmente

# FEDORA/NOBARA (dnf)
sudo dnf install paquete       # instalar
sudo dnf update                # actualizar todo
sudo dnf remove paquete        # desinstalar
sudo dnf search nombre         # buscar
sudo rpm -ivh paquete.rpm      # instalar .rpm

# FLATPAK (universal)
flatpak install flathub app.id  # instalar
flatpak update                 # actualizar todo
flatpak uninstall app.id       # desinstalar
flatpak list                   # listar instalados
flatpak run app.id             # ejecutar app
💻 sistema y hardware
neofetch                   # info del sistema bonita
uname -a                   # info del kernel
lscpu                      # info del CPU
lsmem                      # info de la RAM
lsblk                      # discos y particiones
lsblk -f                   # con filesystem y UUID
lspci                      # dispositivos PCI (GPU etc)
lsusb                      # dispositivos USB
df -h                      # espacio en disco
du -sh carpeta/            # tamaño de carpeta
du -sh g,'.*').replace(/\?/g,'.')+'$'); if(!rx.test(bn)) ok=false; } if(typePat){ if(typePat==='f'&&n.type!=='f') ok=false; if(typePat==='d'&&n.type!=='d') ok=false; } if(ok) results.push(p); if(n.type==='d'&&n.children) n.children.forEach(c=>walk(p==='/'?'/'+c:p+'/'+c)); } walk(startPath); results.slice(0,50).forEach(r=>printText(r)); }; CMD.mkdir = function(args){ const parents=args.includes('-p'); args.filter(a=>!a.startsWith('-')).forEach(d=>{ const p=resolve(d); if(node(p)){ if(!parents)print(`mkdir: cannot create directory '${H(d)}': File exists`); return; } FS[p]={type:'d',perm:'drwxr-xr-x',own:user,grp:user,size:4096,mtime:new Date(),children:[]}; const par=dirOf(p), pn=node(par); if(pn&&pn.children) pn.children.push(basename(p)); }); }; CMD.rmdir = function(args){ args.filter(a=>!a.startsWith('-')).forEach(d=>{ const p=resolve(d), n=node(p); if(!n){ print(`rmdir: failed to remove '${H(d)}': No such file or directory`); return; } if(n.type!=='d'){ print(`rmdir: failed to remove '${H(d)}': Not a directory`); return; } if(n.children&&n.children.length){ print(`rmdir: failed to remove '${H(d)}': Directory not empty`); return; } delete FS[p]; const par=dirOf(p), pn=node(par); if(pn) pn.children=pn.children.filter(c=>c!==basename(p)); }); }; CMD.touch = function(args){ args.filter(a=>!a.startsWith('-')).forEach(f=>{ const p=resolve(f); if(node(p)){ FS[p].mtime=new Date(); return; } FS[p]={type:'f',perm:'-rw-r--r--',own:user,grp:user,size:0,mtime:new Date(),content:''}; const par=dirOf(p), pn=node(par); if(pn&&pn.children) pn.children.push(basename(p)); }); }; CMD.rm = function(args){ const force=args.some(a=>a.includes('f')); const recur=args.some(a=>a.includes('r')||a.includes('R')); const files=args.filter(a=>!a.startsWith('-')); if(!files.length){ print('rm: missing operand'); return; } const protect=['/','//bin','//etc','//usr','//proc','//sys','//dev','//lib','/boot']; files.forEach(f=>{ const p=resolve(f); if(protect.includes(p)){ print(`rm: refusing to remove '${H(f)}': Protected system directory`); return; } const n=node(p); if(!n){ if(!force)print(`rm: cannot remove '${H(f)}': No such file or directory`); return; } if(n.type==='d'&&!recur){ print(`rm: cannot remove '${H(f)}': Is a directory`); return; } function del(pp){ const nd=node(pp); if(!nd)return; if(nd.type==='d'&&nd.children) nd.children.forEach(c=>del(pp==='/'?'/'+c:pp+'/'+c)); delete FS[pp]; } del(p); const par=dirOf(p), pn=node(par); if(pn) pn.children=(pn.children||[]).filter(c=>c!==basename(p)); }); }; CMD.cp = function(args){ const recur=args.some(a=>a.includes('r')||a.includes('R')); const files=args.filter(a=>!a.startsWith('-')); if(files.length<2){ print('cp: missing file operand'); return; } const dst=resolve(files[files.length-1]); files.slice(0,-1).forEach(f=>{ const src=resolve(f), n=node(src); if(!n){ print(`cp: cannot stat '${H(f)}': No such file or directory`); return; } if(n.type==='d'&&!recur){ print(`cp: -r not specified; omitting directory '${H(f)}'`); return; } const dstNode=node(dst); const finalDst=(dstNode&&dstNode.type==='d')?(dst==='/'?'/'+basename(src):dst+'/'+basename(src)):dst; FS[finalDst]={...n, mtime:new Date()}; const par=dirOf(finalDst), pn=node(par); if(pn&&pn.children&&!pn.children.includes(basename(finalDst))) pn.children.push(basename(finalDst)); }); }; CMD.mv = function(args){ const files=args.filter(a=>!a.startsWith('-')); if(files.length<2){ print('mv: missing file operand'); return; } const dst=resolve(files[files.length-1]); files.slice(0,-1).forEach(f=>{ const src=resolve(f), n=node(src); if(!n){ print(`mv: cannot stat '${H(f)}': No such file or directory`); return; } const dstNode=node(dst); const finalDst=(dstNode&&dstNode.type==='d')?(dst==='/'?'/'+basename(src):dst+'/'+basename(src)):dst; FS[finalDst]={...n, mtime:new Date()}; delete FS[src]; const sp=node(dirOf(src)); if(sp) sp.children=(sp.children||[]).filter(c=>c!==basename(src)); const dp=node(dirOf(finalDst)); if(dp&&dp.children&&!dp.children.includes(basename(finalDst))) dp.children.push(basename(finalDst)); }); }; CMD.chmod = function(args){ const mode=args.filter(a=>!a.startsWith('-'))[0]; const files=args.filter(a=>!a.startsWith('-')).slice(1); if(!mode||!files.length){ print('chmod: missing operand'); return; } files.forEach(f=>{ const p=resolve(f), n=node(p); if(!n) print(`chmod: cannot access '${H(f)}': No such file or directory`); }); }; CMD.chown = function(args){ const files=args.filter(a=>!a.startsWith('-')).slice(1); files.forEach(f=>{ const p=resolve(f), n=node(p); if(!n){ print(`chown: cannot access '${H(f)}': No such file or directory`); return; } if(!isRoot) print(`chown: changing ownership of '${H(f)}': Operation not permitted`); }); }; CMD.ln = function(args){ const sym=args.includes('-s'); const files=args.filter(a=>!a.startsWith('-')); if(files.length<2){ print('ln: missing file operand'); return; } const type=sym?'symbolic':'hard'; print(`created ${type} link: ${H(files[1])} -> ${H(files[0])}`); }; CMD.stat = function(args){ const f=args.filter(a=>!a.startsWith('-'))[0]; if(!f){ print('stat: missing operand'); return; } const p=resolve(f), n=node(p); if(!n){ print(`stat: cannot statx '${H(f)}': No such file or directory`); return; } const ino=Math.floor(Math.random()*999999)+100000; printText(` File: ${f}`); printText(` Size: ${n.size||4096}\t\tBlocks: ${Math.ceil((n.size||4096)/512)*8}\t IO Block: 4096 ${n.type==='d'?'directory':'regular file'}`); printText(`Device: 810h/2064d\tInode: ${ino}\tLinks: 1`); printText(`Access: (0${n.perm?n.perm.length:4}/${n.perm||'-rw-r--r--'})\tUid: (${n.own==='root'?0:1000}/${n.own||user})\tGid: (${n.own==='root'?0:1000}/${n.own||user})`); const d=n.mtime||bootDate; const ds=d.toISOString().replace('T',' ').slice(0,19)+' +0000'; printText(`Access: ${ds}`); printText(`Modify: ${ds}`); printText(`Change: ${ds}`); printText(` Birth: ${ds}`); }; CMD.wc = function(args){ const files=args.filter(a=>!a.startsWith('-')); const doL=!args.some(a=>a.match(/^-[^-]/))|| args.some(a=>a.includes('l')); const doW=!args.some(a=>a.match(/^-[^-]/))|| args.some(a=>a.includes('w')); const doC=!args.some(a=>a.match(/^-[^-]/))|| args.some(a=>a.includes('c')); files.forEach(f=>{ const p=resolve(f), n=node(p); if(!n){ print(`wc: ${H(f)}: No such file or directory`); return; } const t=n.content||''; const l=t.split('\n').length, w=t.split(/\s+/).filter(Boolean).length, c=t.length; let out=''; if(doL) out+=` ${l}`; if(doW) out+=` ${w}`; if(doC) out+=` ${c}`; printText(`${out} ${f}`); }); }; CMD.sort = function(args){ const f=args.filter(a=>!a.startsWith('-'))[0]; if(!f){ print('(sort: reading from stdin)'); return; } const n=node(resolve(f)); if(!n){ print(`sort: cannot read: ${H(f)}: No such file or directory`); return; } const lines=(n.content||'').split('\n').filter(Boolean); const rev=args.includes('-r'); lines.sort(); if(rev) lines.reverse(); lines.forEach(l=>printText(l)); }; CMD.uniq = function(args){ const f=args.filter(a=>!a.startsWith('-'))[0]; if(!f){ print('(uniq: reading from stdin)'); return; } const n=node(resolve(f)); if(!n){ print(`uniq: ${H(f)}: No such file or directory`); return; } const lines=(n.content||'').split('\n'); let prev=null; lines.forEach(l=>{ if(l!==prev){ printText(l); prev=l; } }); }; CMD.sed = function(args){ print('sed: stream editing not fully supported in this terminal'); }; CMD.awk = function(args){ print('awk: stream processing not fully supported in this terminal'); }; CMD.diff = function(args){ const files=args.filter(a=>!a.startsWith('-')); if(files.length<2){ print('diff: missing operand'); return; } print(`--- ${H(files[0])}\t2024-11-22 21:00:00.000000000 +0000`); }; CMD.tee = function(args){ print('tee: reading from stdin'); }; CMD.echo = function(args){ let noNL=false, interpret=false; const words=[]; for(const a of args){ if(a==='-n') noNL=true; else if(a==='-e') interpret=true; else if(a==='-ne'||a==='-en'){ noNL=true; interpret=true; } else words.push(a); } let out=words.join(' ').replace(/\$(\w+)/g,(_,v)=>env[v]!==undefined?env[v]:''); out=out.replace(/^["']|["']$/g,''); if(interpret) out=out.replace(/\\n/g,'\n').replace(/\\t/g,'\t'); printText(out); }; CMD.printf = function(args){ printText(args.join(' ').replace(/\\n/g,'\n').replace(/\\t/g,'\t').replace(/^"|"$/g,'')); }; CMD.read = function(){ print('(read: interactive input not supported)'); }; CMD.whoami = function(){ printText(user); }; CMD.id = function(args){ const u = args[0]||user; const u2 = u==='root'; const uidv = u2?0:1000; printText(`uid=${uidv}(${u}) gid=${uidv}(${u}) groups=${uidv}(${u})${u2?'':',10(wheel),92(audio),985(video),998(storage),984(users)'}`); }; CMD.hostname = function(args){ if(args[0]){ host=args[0]; updatePrompt(); } else printText(host); }; CMD.uname = function(args){ const all=args.includes('-a'); if(all||args.includes('-s')||args.length===0) { if(all||args.length===0) { printText(`Linux ${host} 6.12.1-arch1-1 #1 SMP PREEMPT_DYNAMIC Fri, 22 Nov 2024 21:12:22 +0000 x86_64 GNU/Linux`); return; } } if(args.includes('-r')) printText('6.12.1-arch1-1'); else if(args.includes('-m')) printText('x86_64'); else if(args.includes('-n')) printText(host); else if(args.includes('-v')) printText('#1 SMP PREEMPT_DYNAMIC Fri, 22 Nov 2024 21:12:22 +0000'); else if(args.includes('-p')) printText('x86_64'); else if(args.includes('-o')) printText('GNU/Linux'); else if(args.length===0) printText('Linux'); }; CMD.date = function(args){ const now=new Date(); printText(fmt); return; } printText(now.toString()); }; CMD.cal = function(args){ const now=new Date(); const m=now.getMonth(), y=now.getFullYear(); const months=['January','February','March','April','May','June','July','August','September','October','November','December']; if (!canvas) return; const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d'); const W = 80, H = 80, R = 34; let rot = 0; function drawGlobe() { ctx.clearRect(0, 0, W, H); const grad = ctx.createRadialGradient(W/2, H/2, 0, W/2, H/2, R); grad.addColorStop(0, 'rgba(0,100,180,0.25)'); grad.addColorStop(0.7, 'rgba(0,60,120,0.1)'); grad.addColorStop(1, 'rgba(0,220,255,0.05)'); ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(W/2, H/2, R, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fillStyle = grad; ctx.fill(); ctx.save(); ctx.translate(W/2, H/2); for (let lat = -75; lat <= 75; lat += 25) { const y = R * Math.sin(lat * Math.PI/180); const r2 = Math.sqrt(R*R - y*y); ctx.beginPath(); ctx.ellipse(0, y, r2, r2 * 0.25, 0, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(0,220,255,${lat === 0 ? 0.4 : 0.12})`; ctx.lineWidth = lat === 0 ? 0.8 : 0.5; ctx.stroke(); } for (let lon = 0; lon < 180; lon += 30) { const angle = (lon + rot) * Math.PI / 180; ctx.beginPath(); for (let t = 0; t <= Math.PI; t += 0.05) { const x = R * Math.sin(t) * Math.cos(angle); const y2 = -R * Math.cos(t); const vis = Math.cos(angle) > -0.1; if (t === 0) ctx.moveTo(x, y2); else ctx.lineTo(x, y2); } ctx.strokeStyle = `rgba(0,220,255,${Math.abs(Math.cos(angle)) * 0.25 + 0.05})`; ctx.lineWidth = 0.5; ctx.stroke(); } const dots = [ [40, 20], [-20, 60], [10, -30], [60, 100], [-40, 150] ]; dots.forEach(([lat, lon]) => { const a = (lon + rot) * Math.PI/180; const phi = lat * Math.PI/180; const x = R * Math.cos(phi) * Math.cos(a); const y2 = -R * Math.sin(phi); const z = R * Math.cos(phi) * Math.sin(a); if (z > -5) { ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(x, y2, 1.5, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fillStyle = '#00ff9d'; ctx.shadowColor = '#00ff9d'; ctx.shadowBlur = 4; ctx.fill(); ctx.shadowBlur = 0; } }); ctx.restore(); ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(W/2, H/2, R, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,220,255,0.3)'; ctx.lineWidth = 1; ctx.stroke(); ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(W/2, H/2, R+3, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(0,220,255,0.06)'; ctx.lineWidth = 6; ctx.stroke(); rot += 0.4; requestAnimationFrame(drawGlobe); } drawGlobe(); } const _origToggleAdmin = window.toggleAdminPanel; window.toggleAdminPanel = function() { if (_origToggleAdmin) _origToggleAdmin(); let warnCfg = null; if (totalWarns >= 5) warnCfg = cfg.warn5; else if (totalWarns >= 3) warnCfg = cfg.warn3; else if (totalWarns >= 2) warnCfg = cfg.warn2; else if (totalWarns >= 1) warnCfg = cfg.warn1; if (!warnCfg || warnCfg.action === 'nada') return; const action = warnCfg.action; const userRef = window._fbDoc(db, 'users', nick); if (action === 'ban_perm' || action === 'ban_perm_device') { await window._fbUpdateDoc(userRef, { banned: true, banReason: warnCfg.reason || `Auto-ban por ${totalWarns} warns`, }); addLog('AUTO_BAN', `${nick} — ${totalWarns} warns`); showFBToast(`🚫 Auto-ban aplicado a ${nick}`, '#ff4466'); } else if (action.startsWith('ban_')) { await window._fbUpdateDoc(userRef, { banned: true, banReason: warnCfg.reason || `Auto-ban por ${totalWarns} warns`, }); addLog('AUTO_BAN', `${nick} — ${action}`); showFBToast(`🚫 Auto-ban (${action}) aplicado a ${nick}`, '#ff4466'); } else if (action.startsWith('mute_')) { await window._fbUpdateDoc(userRef, { muted: true }); } } } window.loadWarnedUsers = async function() { const el = document.getElementById('warned-users-list'); if (!el) { return; } el.innerHTML = 'cargando...'; try { const snap = await window._fbGetDocs(window._fbCollection(db, 'users')); const warned = []; snap.forEach(d => { const u = d.data(); if ((u.warns || 0) > 0) warned.push(u); }); warned.sort((a, b) => (b.warns || 0) - (a.warns || 0)); if (!warned.length) { el.innerHTML = '✅ nadie tiene warns activos'; ${u.nick}
⚠️ ${u.warns}
`; }).join(''); } catch(e) { el.innerHTML = 'error cargando usuarios'; } }; let _batchTargets = []; // usuarios que serán afectados por el batch window.previewBatch = async function() { const filter = document.getElementById('batch-filter')?.value || 'all_warned'; const previewEl = document.getElementById('batch-preview'); if (previewEl) previewEl.innerHTML = 'buscando...'; try { const snap = await window._fbGetDocs(window._fbCollection(db, 'users')); const allUsers = []; snap.forEach(d => allUsers.push({ id: d.id, ...d.data() })); const now = Date.now(); const day30 = now - 30 * 86400000; const day60 = now - 60 * 86400000; switch(filter) { case 'all_warned': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => (u.warns || 0) >= 1 && !u.admin); break; case 'warned3': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => (u.warns || 0) >= 3 && !u.admin); break; case 'ghosts_30': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => !u.admin && (!u.lastLogin || new Date(u.lastLogin).getTime() < day30)); break; case 'ghosts_60': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => !u.admin && (!u.lastLogin || new Date(u.lastLogin).getTime() < day60)); break; case 'no_login': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => !u.admin && (u.loginCount || 0) === 0); break; case 'muted': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => u.muted && !u.admin); break; case 'banned': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => u.banned && !u.admin); break; case 'rank_user': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => !u.admin && (!u.rank || u.rank === 'user')); break; case 'suspicious': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => (u.tags || []).includes('sospechoso') && !u.admin); break; case 'high_deaths': const deaths = window._fbDeaths || {}; _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => (deaths[u.nick] || 0) > 0 && !u.admin) .sort((a,b) => (deaths[b.nick]||0) - (deaths[a.nick]||0)) .slice(0, 3); break; default: _batchTargets = []; } if (previewEl) { if (!_batchTargets.length) { previewEl.innerHTML = '✅ ningún usuario coincide con este filtro'; } else { previewEl.innerHTML = `
${_batchTargets.length} usuarios afectados:
${_batchTargets.map(u => `${u.nick}` ).join('')} `; } } } catch(e) { if (previewEl) previewEl.innerHTML = 'error al cargar usuarios'; } }; window.executeBatch = async function() { const action = document.getElementById('batch-action')?.value || 'ban'; const reason = (document.getElementById('batch-reason')?.value || '').trim(); const confirmTx = (document.getElementById('batch-confirm-text')?.value || '').trim(); if (!reason) { showFBToast('la razón es obligatoria para batch actions', '#ff4466'); return; } if (confirmTx !== 'CONFIRMAR') { showFBToast('escribe CONFIRMAR para continuar', '#ff9900'); return; } if (!_batchTargets.length) { showFBToast('haz preview primero para ver los afectados', '#ff9900'); return; } if (!hasPermission('batch_actions')) { showFBToast('sin permiso para batch actions', '#ff4466'); return; } const ok = await showConfirm( `Se aplicará "${action}" a ${_batchTargets.length} usuarios. Esta acción no se puede deshacer fácilmente.`, '¿Ejecutar batch action?', '💥' ); if (!ok) return; let count = 0; const errors = []; for (const user of _batchTargets) { try { const ref = window._fbDoc(db, 'users', user.id || user.nick); switch(action) { case 'ban': await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { banned: true, banReason: sanitize(reason) }); break; case 'unban': await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { banned: false, banReason: '' }); break; case 'mute': await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { muted: true }); break; case 'unmute': await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { muted: false }); break; case 'warn': const newWarns = (user.warns || 0) + 1; await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { warns: newWarns }); await applyAutoWarnAction(user.nick, newWarns); break; case 'reset_warns': await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { warns: 0 }); break; case 'tag_suspicious': const tags = [...new Set([...(user.tags || []), 'sospechoso'])]; await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { tags }); break; case 'clear_tags': await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { tags: [] }); break; case 'delete': const { deleteDoc } = await import("https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/11.4.0/firebase-firestore.js"); await deleteDoc(ref); break; } count++; } catch(e) { errors.push(user.nick); console.error(`[Batch] Error en ${user.nick}:`, e); } } const batchHistory = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('papus_batch_history') || '[]'); batchHistory.unshift({ action, reason, count, errors: errors.length, filter: document.getElementById('batch-filter')?.value, time: Date.now(), by: window.currentUser?.nick || 'emilio', }); localStorage.setItem('papus_batch_history', JSON.stringify(batchHistory.slice(0, 50))); addLog('BATCH_' + action.toUpperCase(), `${count} usuarios — ${reason.slice(0, 30)}`); showFBToast(`💥 Batch completado: ${count} ok, ${errors.length} errores`, count > 0 ? '#00ff9d' : '#ff4466'); document.getElementById('batch-confirm-text').value = ''; document.getElementById('batch-reason').value = ''; _batchTargets = []; document.getElementById('batch-preview').innerHTML = ''; loadBatchHistory(); loadUsers(); }; window.clearBatch = function() { _batchTargets = []; const previewEl = document.getElementById('batch-preview'); if (previewEl) previewEl.innerHTML = ''; const confirmEl = document.getElementById('batch-confirm-text'); if (confirmEl) confirmEl.value = ''; const reasonEl = document.getElementById('batch-reason'); if (reasonEl) reasonEl.value = ''; showFBToast('batch cancelado', '#6688aa'); }; window.loadBatchHistory = function() { const el = document.getElementById('batch-history'); if (!el) return; const history = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('papus_batch_history') || '[]'); if (!history.length) { el.innerHTML = 'sin historial'; return; } el.innerHTML = history.slice(0, 20).map(h => `

`; }).join(''); } catch(e) { el.innerHTML = 'error cargando usuarios'; } }; let _batchTargets = []; // usuarios que serán afectados por el batch window.previewBatch = async function() { const filter = document.getElementById('batch-filter')?.value || 'all_warned'; const previewEl = document.getElementById('batch-preview'); if (previewEl) previewEl.innerHTML = 'buscando...'; try { const snap = await window._fbGetDocs(window._fbCollection(db, 'users')); const allUsers = []; snap.forEach(d => allUsers.push({ id: d.id, ...d.data() })); const now = Date.now(); const day30 = now - 30 * 86400000; const day60 = now - 60 * 86400000; switch(filter) { case 'all_warned': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => (u.warns || 0) >= 1 && !u.admin); break; case 'warned3': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => (u.warns || 0) >= 3 && !u.admin); break; case 'ghosts_30': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => !u.admin && (!u.lastLogin || new Date(u.lastLogin).getTime() < day30)); break; case 'ghosts_60': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => !u.admin && (!u.lastLogin || new Date(u.lastLogin).getTime() < day60)); break; case 'no_login': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => !u.admin && (u.loginCount || 0) === 0); break; case 'muted': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => u.muted && !u.admin); break; case 'banned': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => u.banned && !u.admin); break; case 'rank_user': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => !u.admin && (!u.rank || u.rank === 'user')); break; case 'suspicious': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => (u.tags || []).includes('sospechoso') && !u.admin); break; case 'high_deaths': const deaths = window._fbDeaths || {}; _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => (deaths[u.nick] || 0) > 0 && !u.admin) .sort((a,b) => (deaths[b.nick]||0) - (deaths[a.nick]||0)) .slice(0, 3); break; default: _batchTargets = []; } if (previewEl) { if (!_batchTargets.length) { previewEl.innerHTML = '✅ ningún usuario coincide con este filtro'; } else { previewEl.innerHTML = `
${_batchTargets.length} usuarios afectados:
${_batchTargets.map(u => `${u.nick}` ).join('')} `; } } } catch(e) { if (previewEl) previewEl.innerHTML = 'error al cargar usuarios'; } }; window.executeBatch = async function() { const action = document.getElementById('batch-action')?.value || 'ban'; const reason = (document.getElementById('batch-reason')?.value || '').trim(); const confirmTx = (document.getElementById('batch-confirm-text')?.value || '').trim(); if (!reason) { showFBToast('la razón es obligatoria para batch actions', '#ff4466'); return; } if (confirmTx !== 'CONFIRMAR') { showFBToast('escribe CONFIRMAR para continuar', '#ff9900'); return; } if (!_batchTargets.length) { showFBToast('haz preview primero para ver los afectados', '#ff9900'); return; } if (!hasPermission('batch_actions')) { showFBToast('sin permiso para batch actions', '#ff4466'); return; } const ok = await showConfirm( `Se aplicará "${action}" a ${_batchTargets.length} usuarios. Esta acción no se puede deshacer fácilmente.`, '¿Ejecutar batch action?', '💥' ); if (!ok) return; let count = 0; const errors = []; for (const user of _batchTargets) { try { const ref = window._fbDoc(db, 'users', user.id || user.nick); switch(action) { case 'ban': await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { banned: true, banReason: sanitize(reason) }); break; case 'unban': await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { banned: false, banReason: '' }); break; case 'mute': await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { muted: true }); break; case 'unmute': await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { muted: false }); break; case 'warn': const newWarns = (user.warns || 0) + 1; await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { warns: newWarns }); await applyAutoWarnAction(user.nick, newWarns); break; case 'reset_warns': await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { warns: 0 }); break; case 'tag_suspicious': const tags = [...new Set([...(user.tags || []), 'sospechoso'])]; await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { tags }); break; case 'clear_tags': await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { tags: [] }); break; case 'delete': const { deleteDoc } = await import("https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/11.4.0/firebase-firestore.js"); await deleteDoc(ref); break; } count++; } catch(e) { errors.push(user.nick); console.error(`[Batch] Error en ${user.nick}:`, e); } } const batchHistory = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('papus_batch_history') || '[]'); batchHistory.unshift({ action, reason, count, errors: errors.length, filter: document.getElementById('batch-filter')?.value, time: Date.now(), by: window.currentUser?.nick || 'emilio', }); localStorage.setItem('papus_batch_history', JSON.stringify(batchHistory.slice(0, 50))); addLog('BATCH_' + action.toUpperCase(), `${count} usuarios — ${reason.slice(0, 30)}`); showFBToast(`💥 Batch completado: ${count} ok, ${errors.length} errores`, count > 0 ? '#00ff9d' : '#ff4466'); document.getElementById('batch-confirm-text').value = ''; document.getElementById('batch-reason').value = ''; _batchTargets = []; document.getElementById('batch-preview').innerHTML = ''; loadBatchHistory(); loadUsers(); }; window.clearBatch = function() { _batchTargets = []; const previewEl = document.getElementById('batch-preview'); if (previewEl) previewEl.innerHTML = ''; const confirmEl = document.getElementById('batch-confirm-text'); if (confirmEl) confirmEl.value = ''; const reasonEl = document.getElementById('batch-reason'); if (reasonEl) reasonEl.value = ''; showFBToast('batch cancelado', '#6688aa'); }; window.loadBatchHistory = function() { const el = document.getElementById('batch-history'); if (!el) return; const history = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('papus_batch_history') || '[]'); if (!history.length) { el.innerHTML = 'sin historial'; return; } el.innerHTML = history.slice(0, 20).map(h => `

`; }).join(''); } }; const _shortcutsEnabled = { ban: true, warn: true, mute: true, tag: true, log: true, search: true, undo: true, esc: true, }; let _lastAction = null; window.toggleShortcut = function(name, enabled) { _shortcutsEnabled[name] = enabled; localStorage.setItem('papus_shortcuts', JSON.stringify(_shortcutsEnabled)); showFBToast(`Atajo ${name.toUpperCase()} ${enabled ? } catch(e) { return []; } } const TAG_DEFINITIONS = { 'sospechoso': { emoji:'🚨', label:'Sospechoso', bg:'rgba(255,68,102,0.15)', text:'#ff4466', auto: false }, 'toxico': { emoji:'☠️', label:'Tóxico', bg:'rgba(255,100,0,0.15)', text:'#ff6400', auto: false }, 'crack': { emoji:'⭐', label:'Crack', bg:'rgba(255,215,0,0.15)', text:'#ffd700', auto: false }, 'fantasma': { emoji:'👻', label:'Fantasma', bg:'rgba(100,130,180,0.15)', text:'#7ba8d4', auto: false }, 'noob': { emoji:'💀', label:'Noob', bg:'rgba(100,100,100,0.15)', text:'#888888', auto: false }, 'vip': { emoji:'👑', label:'VIP', bg:'rgba(168,85,247,0.15)', text:'#c084fc', auto: false }, 'amigable': { emoji:'😊', label:'Amigable', bg:'rgba(0,255,157,0.12)', text:'#00ff9d', auto: false }, 'scripter': { emoji:'💻', label:'Scripter', bg:'rgba(0,220,255,0.12)', text:'#00dcff', auto: false }, 'auto_top_deaths': { emoji:'💀', label:'Top Muertes', bg:'rgba(255,68,102,0.1)', text:'#ff4466', auto: true }, 'auto_top_toxic': { emoji:'☠️', label:'Más Tóxico', bg:'rgba(255,100,0,0.1)', text:'#ff6400', auto: true }, 'auto_ghost_30': { emoji:'👻', label:'Inactivo 30d', bg:'rgba(80,100,140,0.1)', text:'#6688aa', auto: true }, 'auto_warned': { emoji:'⚠️', label:'Con Warns', bg:'rgba(255,200,0,0.1)', text:'#ffd700', auto: true }, 'auto_newbie': { emoji:'🐣', label:'Recién llegado',bg:'rgba(0,200,100,0.1)', text:'#00cc64', auto: true }, }; }).join(''); } function detectAutoTags(user, deaths, votes) { const autoTags = []; if (user.lastLogin) { const daysSinceLogin = (Date.now() - new Date(user.lastLogin).getTime()) / 86400000; if (daysSinceLogin >= 30 && !user.admin) { autoTags.push('auto_ghost_30'); } } if ((user.warns || 0) >= 2 && !user.admin) { autoTags.push('auto_warned'); } if (user.createdAt) { const daysOld = (Date.now() - user.createdAt) / 86400000; if (daysOld < 3) { autoTags.push('auto_newbie'); } } const userDeaths = deaths ? (deaths[user.nick] || deaths[user.nick?.toLowerCase()] || 0) : 0; if (userDeaths >= 50) { autoTags.push('auto_top_deaths'); } const userVotes = votes ? (votes[user.nick] || votes[user.nick?.toLowerCase()] || 0) : 0; if (userVotes >= 10) { autoTags.push('auto_top_toxic'); } return autoTags; } async function applyAutoTagsToUser(nick, newAutoTags) { try { const snap = await window._fbGetDoc(window._fbDoc(db, 'users', nick)); if (!snap.exists()) return; const currentTags = snap.data().tags || []; const manualTags = currentTags.filter(t => !t.startsWith('auto_')); const finalTags = [...new Set([...manualTags, ...newAutoTags])]; if (JSON.stringify(finalTags.sort()) !== JSON.stringify(currentTags.sort())) { await window._fbUpdateDoc(window._fbDoc(db, 'users', nick), { tags: finalTags }); } } catch(e) { console.warn(`[AutoTags] Error en ${nick}:`, e); } } window.runAutoTagDetection = async function() { if (getRankKey(window.currentUser) !== 'owner') { showFBToast('solo el owner puede ejecutar auto-tag detection', '#ff4466'); return; } showFBToast('⏳ Detectando tags automáticos...', '#00dcff'); try { const usersSnap = await window._fbGetDocs(window._fbCollection(db, 'users')); const deathsSnap = await window._fbGetDoc(window._fbDoc(db, 'lospapus', 'deaths')); const votesSnap = await window._fbGetDoc(window._fbDoc(db, 'lospapus', 'votes')); const deaths = deathsSnap.exists() ? deathsSnap.data() : {}; const votes = votesSnap.exists() ? votesSnap.data() : {}; let processed = 0; for (const doc of usersSnap.docs) { const user = doc.data(); const autoTags = detectAutoTags(user, deaths, votes); await applyAutoTagsToUser(user.nick, autoTags); processed++; } addLog('AUTO_TAGS', `${processed} usuarios procesados`); showFBToast(`✅ Auto-tags aplicados a ${processed} usuarios`, '#00ff9d'); loadUsers(); } catch(e) { showFBToast('Error en auto-tags: ' + e.message, '#ff4466'); } }; function renderTagSelector(currentTags) { const manualTags = Object.entries(TAG_DEFINITIONS).filter(([,def]) => !def.auto); return `

`; } window.toggleTagOnUser = async function(tagId) { const nick = window._currentExpandedUser; if (!nick) { showFBToast('selecciona un usuario primero', '#ff4466'); return; } try { const snap = await window._fbGetDoc(window._fbDoc(db, 'users', nick)); } }; function levenshteinDistance(a, b) { const m = a.length, n = b.length; const dp = Array(m + 1).fill(null).map(() => Array(n + 1).fill(0)); for (let i = 0; i <= m; i++) dp[i][0] = i; for (let j = 0; j <= n; j++) dp[0][j] = j; for (let i = 1; i <= m; i++) { for (let j = 1; j <= n; j++) { if (a[i-1] === b[j-1]) { dp[i][j] = dp[i-1][j-1]; } else { dp[i][j] = 1 + Math.min(dp[i-1][j], dp[i][j-1], dp[i-1][j-1]); } } } return dp[m][n]; } function fuzzySearchUsers(users, query, threshold) { if (!query || !query.trim()) return users; threshold = threshold || 2; const q = query.toLowerCase().trim(); const scored = users.map(user => { const nick = (user.nick || '').toLowerCase(); let score = 0; if (nick === q) score = 100; else if (nick.startsWith(q)) score = 80; else if (nick.includes(q)) score = 60; else { const dist = levenshteinDistance(nick, q); if (dist <= threshold) score = Math.max(0, 40 - dist * 15); } return { user, score }; }); return scored .filter(s => s.score > 0) .sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score) .map(s => s.user); } function debounce(func, wait) { let timeout; return function executedFunction(...args) { clearTimeout(timeout); timeout = setTimeout(() => func.apply(this, args), wait); }; } const debouncedUserSearch = debounce(function(query) { if (window._allUsersCache && window._allUsersCache.length > 0) { const results = fuzzySearchUsers(window._allUsersCache, query); if (ms < 3600000) return `hace ${Math.floor(ms/60000)} min`; if (ms < 86400000) return `hace ${Math.floor(ms/3600000)}h`; if (ms < 2592000000) return `hace ${Math.floor(ms/86400000)} días`; return new Date(timestamp).toLocaleDateString('es'); } function validateNick(nick) { if (!nick) return { valid: false, error: 'El nick no puede estar vacío' }; if (nick.length < 3) return { valid: false, error: 'El nick debe tener al menos 3 caracteres' }; `; }).join(''); } catch(e) { el.innerHTML = 'error cargando usuarios'; } }; let _batchTargets = []; // usuarios que serán afectados por el batch window.previewBatch = async function() { const filter = document.getElementById('batch-filter')?.value || 'all_warned'; const previewEl = document.getElementById('batch-preview'); if (previewEl) previewEl.innerHTML = 'buscando...'; try { const snap = await window._fbGetDocs(window._fbCollection(db, 'users')); const allUsers = []; snap.forEach(d => allUsers.push({ id: d.id, ...d.data() })); const now = Date.now(); const day30 = now - 30 * 86400000; const day60 = now - 60 * 86400000; switch(filter) { case 'all_warned': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => (u.warns || 0) >= 1 && !u.admin); break; case 'warned3': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => (u.warns || 0) >= 3 && !u.admin); break; case 'ghosts_30': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => !u.admin && (!u.lastLogin || new Date(u.lastLogin).getTime() < day30)); break; case 'ghosts_60': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => !u.admin && (!u.lastLogin || new Date(u.lastLogin).getTime() < day60)); break; case 'no_login': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => !u.admin && (u.loginCount || 0) === 0); break; case 'muted': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => u.muted && !u.admin); break; case 'banned': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => u.banned && !u.admin); break; case 'rank_user': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => !u.admin && (!u.rank || u.rank === 'user')); break; case 'suspicious': _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => (u.tags || []).includes('sospechoso') && !u.admin); break; case 'high_deaths': const deaths = window._fbDeaths || {}; _batchTargets = allUsers.filter(u => (deaths[u.nick] || 0) > 0 && !u.admin) .sort((a,b) => (deaths[b.nick]||0) - (deaths[a.nick]||0)) .slice(0, 3); break; default: _batchTargets = []; } if (previewEl) { if (!_batchTargets.length) { previewEl.innerHTML = '✅ ningún usuario coincide con este filtro'; } else { previewEl.innerHTML = `
${_batchTargets.length} usuarios afectados:
${_batchTargets.map(u => `${u.nick}` ).join('')} `; } } } catch(e) { if (previewEl) previewEl.innerHTML = 'error al cargar usuarios'; } }; window.executeBatch = async function() { const action = document.getElementById('batch-action')?.value || 'ban'; const reason = (document.getElementById('batch-reason')?.value || '').trim(); const confirmTx = (document.getElementById('batch-confirm-text')?.value || '').trim(); if (!reason) { showFBToast('la razón es obligatoria para batch actions', '#ff4466'); return; } if (confirmTx !== 'CONFIRMAR') { showFBToast('escribe CONFIRMAR para continuar', '#ff9900'); return; } if (!_batchTargets.length) { showFBToast('haz preview primero para ver los afectados', '#ff9900'); return; } if (!hasPermission('batch_actions')) { showFBToast('sin permiso para batch actions', '#ff4466'); return; } const ok = await showConfirm( `Se aplicará "${action}" a ${_batchTargets.length} usuarios. Esta acción no se puede deshacer fácilmente.`, '¿Ejecutar batch action?', '💥' ); if (!ok) return; let count = 0; const errors = []; for (const user of _batchTargets) { try { const ref = window._fbDoc(db, 'users', user.id || user.nick); switch(action) { case 'ban': await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { banned: true, banReason: sanitize(reason) }); break; case 'unban': await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { banned: false, banReason: '' }); break; case 'mute': await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { muted: true }); break; case 'unmute': await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { muted: false }); break; case 'warn': const newWarns = (user.warns || 0) + 1; await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { warns: newWarns }); await applyAutoWarnAction(user.nick, newWarns); break; case 'reset_warns': await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { warns: 0 }); break; case 'tag_suspicious': const tags = [...new Set([...(user.tags || []), 'sospechoso'])]; await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { tags }); break; case 'clear_tags': await window._fbUpdateDoc(ref, { tags: [] }); break; case 'delete': const { deleteDoc } = await import("https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/11.4.0/firebase-firestore.js"); await deleteDoc(ref); break; } count++; } catch(e) { errors.push(user.nick); console.error(`[Batch] Error en ${user.nick}:`, e); } } const batchHistory = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('papus_batch_history') || '[]'); batchHistory.unshift({ action, reason, count, errors: errors.length, filter: document.getElementById('batch-filter')?.value, time: Date.now(), by: window.currentUser?.nick || 'emilio', }); localStorage.setItem('papus_batch_history', JSON.stringify(batchHistory.slice(0, 50))); addLog('BATCH_' + action.toUpperCase(), `${count} usuarios — ${reason.slice(0, 30)}`); showFBToast(`💥 Batch completado: ${count} ok, ${errors.length} errores`, count > 0 ? '#00ff9d' : '#ff4466'); document.getElementById('batch-confirm-text').value = ''; document.getElementById('batch-reason').value = ''; _batchTargets = []; document.getElementById('batch-preview').innerHTML = ''; loadBatchHistory(); loadUsers(); }; window.clearBatch = function() { _batchTargets = []; const previewEl = document.getElementById('batch-preview'); if (previewEl) previewEl.innerHTML = ''; const confirmEl = document.getElementById('batch-confirm-text'); if (confirmEl) confirmEl.value = ''; const reasonEl = document.getElementById('batch-reason'); if (reasonEl) reasonEl.value = ''; showFBToast('batch cancelado', '#6688aa'); }; window.loadBatchHistory = function() { const el = document.getElementById('batch-history'); if (!el) return; const history = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('papus_batch_history') || '[]'); if (!history.length) { el.innerHTML = 'sin historial'; return; } el.innerHTML = history.slice(0, 20).map(h => `

`; }).join(''); } }; const _shortcutsEnabled = { ban: true, warn: true, mute: true, tag: true, log: true, search: true, undo: true, esc: true, }; let _lastAction = null; window.toggleShortcut = function(name, enabled) { _shortcutsEnabled[name] = enabled; localStorage.setItem('papus_shortcuts', JSON.stringify(_shortcutsEnabled)); showFBToast(`Atajo ${name.toUpperCase()} ${enabled ? } catch(e) { return []; } } const TAG_DEFINITIONS = { 'sospechoso': { emoji:'🚨', label:'Sospechoso', bg:'rgba(255,68,102,0.15)', text:'#ff4466', auto: false }, 'toxico': { emoji:'☠️', label:'Tóxico', bg:'rgba(255,100,0,0.15)', text:'#ff6400', auto: false }, 'crack': { emoji:'⭐', label:'Crack', bg:'rgba(255,215,0,0.15)', text:'#ffd700', auto: false }, 'fantasma': { emoji:'👻', label:'Fantasma', bg:'rgba(100,130,180,0.15)', text:'#7ba8d4', auto: false }, 'noob': { emoji:'💀', label:'Noob', bg:'rgba(100,100,100,0.15)', text:'#888888', auto: false }, 'vip': { emoji:'👑', label:'VIP', bg:'rgba(168,85,247,0.15)', text:'#c084fc', auto: false }, 'amigable': { emoji:'😊', label:'Amigable', bg:'rgba(0,255,157,0.12)', text:'#00ff9d', auto: false }, 'scripter': { emoji:'💻', label:'Scripter', bg:'rgba(0,220,255,0.12)', text:'#00dcff', auto: false }, 'auto_top_deaths': { emoji:'💀', label:'Top Muertes', bg:'rgba(255,68,102,0.1)', text:'#ff4466', auto: true }, 'auto_top_toxic': { emoji:'☠️', label:'Más Tóxico', bg:'rgba(255,100,0,0.1)', text:'#ff6400', auto: true }, 'auto_ghost_30': { emoji:'👻', label:'Inactivo 30d', bg:'rgba(80,100,140,0.1)', text:'#6688aa', auto: true }, 'auto_warned': { emoji:'⚠️', label:'Con Warns', bg:'rgba(255,200,0,0.1)', text:'#ffd700', auto: true }, 'auto_newbie': { emoji:'🐣', label:'Recién llegado',bg:'rgba(0,200,100,0.1)', text:'#00cc64', auto: true }, }; function renderUserTagBadges(tags, compact) { if (!tags || !tags.length) return ''; return tags.map(tagId => { const def = TAG_DEFINITIONS[tagId]; if (!def) { return ` ${tagId} `; } return ` ${def.emoji} ${compact?'':def.label} `; }).join(''); } function detectAutoTags(user, deaths, votes) { const autoTags = []; if (user.lastLogin) { const daysSinceLogin = (Date.now() - new Date(user.lastLogin).getTime()) / 86400000; if (daysSinceLogin >= 30 && !user.admin) { autoTags.push('auto_ghost_30'); } } if ((user.warns || 0) >= 2 && !user.admin) { autoTags.push('auto_warned'); } if (user.createdAt) { const daysOld = (Date.now() - user.createdAt) / 86400000; if (daysOld < 3) { autoTags.push('auto_newbie'); } } const userDeaths = deaths ? (deaths[user.nick] || deaths[user.nick?.toLowerCase()] || 0) : 0; if (userDeaths >= 50) { autoTags.push('auto_top_deaths'); } const userVotes = votes ? (votes[user.nick] || votes[user.nick?.toLowerCase()] || 0) : 0; if (userVotes >= 10) { autoTags.push('auto_top_toxic'); } return autoTags; } async function applyAutoTagsToUser(nick, newAutoTags) { try { const snap = await window._fbGetDoc(window._fbDoc(db, 'users', nick)); if (!snap.exists()) return; const currentTags = snap.data().tags || []; const manualTags = currentTags.filter(t => !t.startsWith('auto_')); const finalTags = [...new Set([...manualTags, ...newAutoTags])]; if (JSON.stringify(finalTags.sort()) !== JSON.stringify(currentTags.sort())) { await window._fbUpdateDoc(window._fbDoc(db, 'users', nick), { tags: finalTags }); } } catch(e) { console.warn(`[AutoTags] Error en ${nick}:`, e); } } window.runAutoTagDetection = async function() { if (getRankKey(window.currentUser) !== 'owner') { showFBToast('solo el owner puede ejecutar auto-tag detection', '#ff4466'); return; } showFBToast('⏳ Detectando tags automáticos...', '#00dcff'); try { const usersSnap = await window._fbGetDocs(window._fbCollection(db, 'users')); const deathsSnap = await window._fbGetDoc(window._fbDoc(db, 'lospapus', 'deaths')); const votesSnap = await window._fbGetDoc(window._fbDoc(db, 'lospapus', 'votes')); const deaths = deathsSnap.exists() ? deathsSnap.data() : {}; const votes = votesSnap.exists() ? votesSnap.data() : {}; let processed = 0; for (const doc of usersSnap.docs) { const user = doc.data(); const autoTags = detectAutoTags(user, deaths, votes); await applyAutoTagsToUser(user.nick, autoTags); processed++; } addLog('AUTO_TAGS', `${processed} usuarios procesados`); showFBToast(`✅ Auto-tags aplicados a ${processed} usuarios`, '#00ff9d'); loadUsers(); } catch(e) { showFBToast('Error en auto-tags: ' + e.message, '#ff4466'); } }; function renderTagSelector(currentTags) { const manualTags = Object.entries(TAG_DEFINITIONS).filter(([,def]) => !def.auto); return `

`; } window.toggleTagOnUser = async function(tagId) { const nick = window._currentExpandedUser; if (!nick) { showFBToast('selecciona un usuario primero', '#ff4466'); return; } try { const snap = await window._fbGetDoc(window._fbDoc(db, 'users', nick)); } }; function levenshteinDistance(a, b) { const m = a.length, n = b.length; const dp = Array(m + 1).fill(null).map(() => Array(n + 1).fill(0)); for (let i = 0; i <= m; i++) dp[i][0] = i; for (let j = 0; j <= n; j++) dp[0][j] = j; for (let i = 1; i <= m; i++) { for (let j = 1; j <= n; j++) { if (a[i-1] === b[j-1]) { dp[i][j] = dp[i-1][j-1]; } else { dp[i][j] = 1 + Math.min(dp[i-1][j], dp[i][j-1], dp[i-1][j-1]); } } } return dp[m][n]; } function fuzzySearchUsers(users, query, threshold) { if (!query || !query.trim()) return users; threshold = threshold || 2; const q = query.toLowerCase().trim(); const scored = users.map(user => { const nick = (user.nick || '').toLowerCase(); let score = 0; if (nick === q) score = 100; else if (nick.startsWith(q)) score = 80; else if (nick.includes(q)) score = 60; else { const dist = levenshteinDistance(nick, q); if (dist <= threshold) score = Math.max(0, 40 - dist * 15); } return { user, score }; }); return scored .filter(s => s.score > 0) .sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score) .map(s => s.user); } function debounce(func, wait) { let timeout; return function executedFunction(...args) { clearTimeout(timeout); timeout = setTimeout(() => func.apply(this, args), wait); }; } const debouncedUserSearch = debounce(function(query) { if (window._allUsersCache && window._allUsersCache.length > 0) { const results = fuzzySearchUsers(window._allUsersCache, query); 'es' : ''}`; if (days > 0) return `${days} día${days > 1 ? 's' : ''}`; if (hours > 0) return `${hours} hora${hours > 1 ? 's' : ''}`; if (minutes > 0) return `${minutes} min`; return `${seconds}s`; } function timeAgo(timestamp) { if (!timestamp) return 'nunca'; const ms = Date.now() - timestamp; if (ms < 60000) return 'hace un momento'; if (ms < 3600000) return `hace ${Math.floor(ms/60000)} min`; if (ms < 86400000) return `hace ${Math.floor(ms/3600000)}h`; if (ms < 2592000000) return `hace ${Math.floor(ms/86400000)} días`; return new Date(timestamp).toLocaleDateString('es'); } function validateNick(nick) { if (!nick) return { valid: false, error: 'El nick no puede estar vacío' }; if (nick.length < 3) return { valid: false, error: 'El nick debe tener al menos 3 caracteres' }; if (nick.length > 16) return { valid: false, error: 'El nick no puede tener más de 16 caracteres' }; if (!/^[a-zA-Z0-9_-]+$/.test(nick)) { return { valid: false, error: 'Solo letras, números, _ y - están permitidos' };
